			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;In times like these </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">I like to remind </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">stakeholders </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> see the forest </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">through</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the trees.&nbsp;&nbsp;We continue to be a business with a very strong moat, diversified across many trade channels and countries around the world.&nbsp;&nbsp;We have a strong balance sheet, generate steady cash flow</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, and continue to return capital to our investors though regular dividends.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, the WD-40&#xAE; Brand is strong and robust brands</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> like ours</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> are great assets in turbulent times. Most critical of all, we have passionate and committed employees who are dedicated to our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">C</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ompany&#x2019;s purpose.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As we look to the remainder of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fiscal year, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">despite the global disruptions we&#x2019;ve experienced, we </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">continue to believe we are positioned to achieve sales growth for the full fiscal year which will represent a record sales result for our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Company</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; Ridge concluded.</font>

Higher sales of maintenance products in Canada were primarily due to increased promotional activities and a higher level </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">of demand for our products in the industrial channel.&nbsp;&nbsp;Higher sales of maintenance products in Latin America were primarily driven by strong sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in Mexico due to the continued momentum from the shift in the Mexico market from a distributor model to the direct model that we made in late fiscal year 2020.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In addition, price increases that went into effect earlier this fiscal year had a positive impact on sales in the region. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In the United States, sales remained relatively constant period over period.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Th</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ese</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">decreases were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily attributable to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">lower</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">maintenance products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the Company&#x2019;s China and Asia-Pacific distributor markets due to lockdown measures in Shanghai related to the COVID-19 pandemic that severely limited our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ability to ship product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the region</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. Also contributing to the decline was the Company&#x2019;s suspension of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales in Russia due to the ongoing impacts of the Russian </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">m</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ilitary action in Ukraine</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Finally, sales were lower in the Company&#x2019;s EMEA direct markets due to reduced demand and changing foreign currency exchange rates compared to the prior year period.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">third </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> when compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> homecare and cleaning products, particularly </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">those </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the U</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">nited States</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, are considered harvest brands providing healthy profits to the Company and are becoming a smaller part of the business as net sales of maintenance products grow</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, reflecting</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the execution of the Company&#x2019;s strategic initiatives.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company owns a wide range of well-known brands that include maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products: WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Multi-Use Product, WD-40 Specialist</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 3-IN-ONE</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, GT85</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 2000 Flushes</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, no vac</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 1001</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Spot Shot</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Lava&#xAE;, Solvol</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, X-14</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, and Carpet Fresh</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $488.1 million in fiscal year 2021 and its products are currently available in more than </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">176</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit http://www.wd40company.com.</font>
		</p>
